-- Dumping structure for table fun_world.eluna_counters
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `eluna_counters` (
  `value_1` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `value_2` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `script_name` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='random counters logged for eluna\r\n---\r\nval1 = 1st value logged\r\n---\r\nscript_name = name of script that refers here';

-- Data exporting was unselected.

-- Dumping structure for table fun_world.eluna_mythiclite_affixes_pool
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `eluna_mythiclite_affixes_pool` (
  `spellID` int DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci COMMENT='spellID = spellID of the affix that was generated for the pool';

-- Data exporting was unselected.

-- Dumping structure for table fun_world.eluna_mythiclite_affixes_template
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `eluna_mythiclite_affixes_template` (
  `spellID` int NOT NULL,
  `base_stack` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `stack_per_level` int DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`spellID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci COMMENT='spellID, base_stack, stack_per_level';

-- Data exporting was unselected.

-- Dumping structure for table fun_world.eluna_mythiclite_keystones
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `eluna_mythiclite_keystones` (
  `itemGUID` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `playerGUID` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `mythicLevel` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `mapID` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `affixString` varchar(499) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `timestamp` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `progress` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `instanceID` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `bosses` int DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci COMMENT='itemGUID, playerGUID, mythicLevel, mapID, affixString, timestamp, progress, instanceID, lastboss\r\nAffix String = our "list" of affixes\r\ntimestamp = when we start the mythic dungeon\r\nprogress = how far a mythic has progressed. This is determined in a percentage 0-100.\r\ninstanceID = the ID of the dungeon that keystone will be consumed in.\r\nbosses = a whole integer storing the real progress of boss kills';

-- Data exporting was unselected.

-- Dumping structure for table fun_world.eluna_mythiclite_progress
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `eluna_mythiclite_progress` (
  `creatureGUID` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `instanceID` int DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci COMMENT='saves progress data of each keystone dungeon. if a mob is in here, it means that it is considered killed for the progress of the dungeon.';

-- Data exporting was unselected.

-- Dumping structure for table fun_world.eluna_mythiclite_records
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `eluna_mythiclite_records` (
  `itemGUID` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `mythicLevel` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `mapID` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `duration` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `affixString` varchar(499) DEFAULT NULL,
  `player1` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `player2` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `player3` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `player4` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `player5` int DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci COMMENT='holds logs of completed mythic dungeons';

-- Data exporting was unselected.

-- Dumping structure for table fun_world.eluna_mythiclite_template
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `eluna_mythiclite_template` (
  `mapID` int NOT NULL,
  `timelimit` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `totalMod` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `dungeonName` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`mapID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci COMMENT='mapID = mapID of the dungeon\r\nlastBossID = creature ID of the final boss\r\ntimelimit = amount of time it would take to clear this dungeon, in seconds\r\ntotalMobs= amount of creatures total detected for this dungeon. find these in-game by typing ".mythiclite" as a GM and while on said map.\r\ntotalMod= if you want 100% clear you would make this 100. If you want 50% clear required, you would make this 50.\r\ndungeonName = never sent to the client. just a comment for db reading.';

-- Data exporting was unselected.

-- Dumping structure for table fun_world.eluna_mythiclite_template_mobs
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `eluna_mythiclite_template_mobs` (
  `guid` int NOT NULL,
  `mapID` int DEFAULT NULL,
  UNIQUE KEY `guid` (`guid`),
  KEY `mapID` (`mapID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci COMMENT='saves GUID info in relation to the mapID. if you need to manually add a creature to the progression list for whatever reason, this is how you would do it.';
